 The number of HIV positive patients in Sindh province has become uncontrollable
 taaja aankadon ke mutabik sindh praant ke larkana or ratodero shaharon main 700 log echivi positive paae gaye hai
 The surprising thing is that out of 700 HIV positive patients, 576 are children
 iskaa matabal yah he ki ye aankada or bhi bad saktaa he
 Seeing such a large number of HIV patients, the world's health agencies are also frightened
 WHO, UNICEF or UNAIDS jaise sansthaaen apane pratinidhi pakistan bhej rahe hai
 Representatives of these institutions are coming to Karachi to find out the root cause of the spread of HIV
 karachi aane vaale international export main vishwa swasthya sanghathan, centre for dijis control, unicef, aneds ke adhikari shaamil hai
 An official said that a team of 12 experts led by Dr
 Oliver Morgan, director of the World Health Organization's Health Emergency and Risk Assessment, has reached Karachi
 report ke mutabik injection dene vaale syringe kaa dobaaraa istemaal, blad transfusion ke equipment kii kami larkana or ratodero main echivi ke failane kaa mukhya kaaran he

 In winter this year, influenza increased in many parts of India due to type A, subtype H1N1 virus or swine flu
 yah vahi virus he jisase 2009 main duniyabar main mahamari fail gai thi
 It continued to spread in 2010 as well, remaining sluggish for a few years thereafter and intermittently in 2013
 farvari 2014 main vishwa swasthya sanghathan (dablyuechao) ne ghoshit kiya ki is virus ko mausami influenza strain mana jaae
 In other words, the virus is no different from other seasonal flu viruses (such as a / H3N2 or B), which spread regularly throughout each season of influenza
 2014 main influenza kam sakriy tha
 a / H1N1 was not seen very much
 balki 2011 ke baad se, influenza virus e / ech3en2 or influenza bi zyada prabhavi rahe
 But when a particular influenza virus spreads over a long period of time, most individuals develop immunity from it
 iske baad, koi anya mausami strain logon ko sankramit karnaa shuru kar detaa he
 This cyclical pattern is typical of seasonal influenza
 influenza kaa mukhya mausam monsoon ke saath aata he
 Occasionally, the activity of influenza virus increases even in the cold season, with a slight peak in january-march
 ghabaraaen nahipune ke rashtriya vishaanu vigyaan santhaan ne jin seqvencing se pushti kii he ki is saal faile e / ech1en1 influenza virus main koi mahatvapurn parivartan nahin hua he
 Current vaccines should prevent disease, and existing antiviral drugs (eg, oseltamivir) are still effective
 adhikansh rogiyon main influenza ke virus kii vajah se (influenza e / ech1en1 strain sahit) khaansee yaa gale kii kharash ke saath sirf halkaa bukhaar hota he
 The disease lasts for a few days, after which most patients recover without the need for testing or treatment
 zyada jokhim kahaan haphir bhi, sabhi influenza virus, bhale hi unka tip or sab-tip kuch bhi ho, (influenza e / ech1en1 ho athwa e / ech3en2 yaa bi ho) kuch zyada jokhim vaale samoohon main gambhir beemaari paidaa kar sakate hai
 High-risk individuals include the elderly (those above 60 years of age), children below five years of age already with a risk factor (eg, asthma), pregnant women, and effects on the lungs, kidneys, or heart
 People who have been suffering from long-term dangerous diseases are involved
 isamen ve log bhi shaamil hai, jinaki jaanch main madhumeh, pratirohak kshamta kii kami (jaise, echivi sankraman, lambey samay tak steroid upachaar) yaa cancer paaya gaya ho

 According to the official statement released on Saturday, foreign investment in the retail business will create one crore jobs and out of this, 60 lakh jobs will be created only in the field of freight and maintenance
 sharma ne kaha ki niti tay karte samay desh ke kisaanon or yuvaaon ke hiton kaa dhyaan rakhaa gaya he

 ' An asthma attack during pregnancy is a serious condition for any woman, so women should be tested for asthma early in pregnancy
 uchit samay par asthma kaa ilaaj na kiya jaae to mahila or hone vaale bachche donon kii jaan khatre main pad sakati he
 JP Hospital Noida Senior Consultant Respiratory Medicine Dr
 gyanendra agarwal ne kaha, "garbhavastha ke dauraan mahilaon ko ucch raktchaap kii samasya or urine main protein kii maatra bad jaati he
 With this, the fetus starts feeling deficient in oxygen
 iske liye mahilaon ko apni asthma ke dawaaen leti rahani chahie or lagaataar doctor ke sampark main rahanaa chahie
 In addition, during pregnancy, dust, dirt, smoke and odor etc
 should be kept away from allergic things
 "ek study ke anusaar 10 pratishat dama peedit mahilaon ko pregnent hone main saamaanya mahilaon kii tulana main zyada samay lagata he
 Dr
 Satish Kaul, Director of Internal Medicine, Naraina Superspeciality Hospital, Gurugram, said, "in asthma patients the respiratory tract gets inflamed, causing the windpipe to shrink, which causes them to have trouble breathing
 bharat main lagaataar asthma ke rogiyon kii sankhya badhati ja rahi he, yahaan lagbhag 20-30 million log asthma se peedit he
 To avoid this, it is important to first identify whether the symptoms you see are asthma or not
 aisa isliye kyonki har baar saans phoolnaa asthma nahin hota he, lekin agar kisi ko asthma he to uski saans jarur phoolati he
 In asthma patients, symptoms of breathlessness, whistling while breathing, coughing for a long time, complaining of chest pain and chest tightness are seen
 is rog kii sahi pahchaan ke liye pulmonary function test anivaary he
 "dharmashila Narayana Super Specialty Hospital's Consultant Pulmonology Dr
 navaneet sood ne kaha, "asthma se peedit adhikansh vyakti ko inhiler prayog karne se phayda nahin mil paata, jiskaa kaaran inhiler kaa galat tareeke se prayog karnaa hota he
 If the inhaler is not used properly, the drug particles do not reach the windpipe, due to which the medicine remains in the throat, it does not provide comfort to the patient
 "unhone kaha ki ek research ke anusaar inhiler ke galat istemaal ke kaaran gale main dawa ke kan ikatthe hone se gale ke cancer hone kaa khatra bhi hota he isliye inhiler kaa sahi dhang se prayog karnaa jaruri he
 Asthma sufferers should not open the mouth immediately while using an inhaler, so that the drug particles can reach the lungs directly
 iske saath hi inhiler istemaal karne kaa sahi tarika hameshaa doctor se check karaate rahen, jisase asthma ko niyantrit karne main madad mil saken
 Balaji Action Medical Institute Senior Consultant Respiratory Medicine Dr
 jnyandeep mangal ke anusaar, "asthma kii beemaari sabhi aayu varg ke vyaktiyon main kabhi bhi ho sakati he
 Asthma disease can also be caused by genetic reasons
 agar mata-pita main se kisi ek yaa donon ko asthma he to bachein main iske hone kii ashanka bad jaati he
 In addition, air pollution, smoking, dust, smoke and incense sticks are among the main causes of asthma disease
 "unhone kaha, "vishwa swasthya sanghathan ke anusaar duniyabar main lagbhag 33
 90 million people are affected by asthma, of which 2-3 crore people in India have asthma
